    2674                 :           0 : static int check_trailing_bits_after_symbol_coder(aom_reader *r) {
    2675                 :           0 :   if (aom_reader_has_overflowed(r)) return -1;
    2676                 :             : 
    2677                 :           0 :   uint32_t nb_bits = aom_reader_tell(r);
    2678                 :           0 :   uint32_t nb_bytes = (nb_bits + 7) >> 3;
    2679                 :           0 :   const uint8_t *p = aom_reader_find_begin(r) + nb_bytes;
    2680                 :             : 
    2681                 :             :   // aom_reader_tell() returns 1 for a newly initialized decoder, and the
    2682                 :             :   // return value only increases as values are decoded. So nb_bits > 0, and
    2683                 :             :   // thus p > p_begin. Therefore accessing p[-1] is safe.
    2684                 :           0 :   uint8_t last_byte = p[-1];
    2685                 :           0 :   uint8_t pattern = 128 >> ((nb_bits - 1) & 7);
    2686                 :           0 :   if ((last_byte & (2 * pattern - 1)) != pattern) return -1;
    2687                 :             : 
    2688                 :             :   // Make sure that all padding bytes are zero as required by the spec.
    2689                 :           0 :   const uint8_t *p_end = aom_reader_find_end(r);
    2690                 :           0 :   while (p < p_end) {
    2691                 :           0 :     if (*p != 0) return -1;
    2692                 :           0 :     p++;
    2693                 :             :   }
    2694                 :           0 :   return 0;
    2695                 :           0 : }
